No. 1049 They had words again yesterday, so they're not speaking today. (1) had a quarrel (2) had a chat (3) had a discussion (4) had a speech <駒澤大>
1049 have words (with A) 「(Aと)口論をする」
= have a quarrel (with A) [標準]

No. 1050 The boys get on my nerves with that noise they make. (1) amuse me (2) irritate me (3) surprise me (4) encourage me <青山学院大>
1050 get on A's nerves 「Aの神経にさわる」
= irritate A [発展]
No. 1051 We had better not make too much ( ) this incident. 〈中央大〉
① of ② in ③ to ④ for
Point 187 その他の動詞を含む重要イディオム 1051 make much of A「Aを重視する」＋プラス 反意表現の make light[little] of A「Aを軽視する」も重要。He made light of the difficulty he would possibly encounter.（彼は、直面する可能性のある困難さを軽視した）標準

No. 1052 Those young girls don't ( ) fashion. 〈札博学院大〉
① think much of ② look like ③ do away with ④ hold back from
1052 think much of A「Aを重視する」= think highly of A, make much of A (→1051) 標準 ＋プラス think little of A「Aを軽視する」= think light of A, make light[little] of A (→1051) もここで押さえよう。

No. 1053 John was about to say something more, but then he seemed to ( ) better of it. 〈立教大〉
① know ② see ③ sense ④ think
1053 think better of A「Aを考え直す」= have second thoughts about A 標準

No. 1054 When Tom ate dessert with his fingers, his father told him to ( ) himself. 〈神田外大〉
① act ② do ③ behave ④ get
1054 behave oneself「行儀よくする」標準

No. 1055 I don't know ( ) with these books. Please tell me where to put them. 〈流通科学大〉
① what to do ② where to be done ③ how to do ④ how come
1055 what ... do with A「Aをどう処理するか／扱うか」▶本問は「疑問詞＋to不定詞」の形となっている点に注意。標準

No. 1056 ( ) to it that this letter gets posted today. 〈昭和女子大〉
① Glance ② Watch ③ See ④ View
1056 see (to it) that 節「…するように取り計らう」標準

No. 1057 When you leave your room, please ( ) sure that the door is locked. 〈千葉商科大〉
① do ② get ③ have ④ make
1057 make sure that 節「…を確かめる」＋プラス make sure of A「Aを確かめる」もここで押さえる。Search your pockets again to make sure of it.（それがあるか確かめるために、もう一度ポケットの中を調べなさい）標準

No. 1058 His composition ( ) much to be desired. 〈国士舘大〉
① appears ② grows ③ leaves ④ throws
1058 leave much to be desired「改善の余地がかなりある」⇔ leave nothing to be desired「申し分ない」▶to be desired は形容詞用法の不定詞。leave much to be desired「望まれる点をたくさん残している」、leave nothing to be desired「望まれる点を何も残していない」という本来の意味から上記の訳語になる。標準

No. 1059 This letter will ( ) home to you how much she loves you. 〈聖心女子大〉
① lead ② read ③ bring ④ feel
1059 bring[drive] A home to B「AのことをBにしみじみわからせる」発展 ▶本問のように、目的語のAが移動して bring[drive] home to B Aという形になることが多い。＋プラス come home to A「Aにしみじみわかる」もここで押さえる。

No. 1060 Do you see ( ) of him these days? 〈京都産大〉
① least ② many ③ most ④ much
1060 see much of A「Aによく会う」▶通例、疑問文・否定文で用いる。

No. 1061 My brother wanted to ( ) on working until he was 65. 〈中央大〉
① keep ② continue ③ get ④ step
1061 keep on doing「…し続ける」= continue doing

No. 1062 Bob made believe that he was very hungry. 〈江戸川大〉
① pretended ② convinced ③ firmly believed ④ was afraid
1062 make believe that 節「…のふりをする」= pretend that 節 !!注意 make believe は目的語に that 節または不定詞をとる。標準

No. 1063 Why don't you avail yourself of the free classes to improve your English? 〈獨協大〉
① enjoy ② devote yourself to ③ get ④ make use of
1063 avail oneself of A「Aを利用する」= take advantage of A (→782), make use of A (→997) 標準

No. 1064 This rule holds good at all times and places. 〈立命館大〉
① is made much of ② is thought highly of ③ is valid ④ is practical
1064 hold good「有効である」= be valid 標準

No. 1065 He made the most of his limited space in the dormitory when he was a college student. 〈立命館大〉
① enjoyed very much ② created nearly all of ③ decorated beautifully ④ utilized effectively
1065 make the most of A「Aを最大限に利用する」!!注意 よく似た表現に make the best of A「A（不利な状況）を精一杯利用する／とかくうまく切り抜ける」があるが、意味の違いを正確にしておくこと。I didn't want to work with her, but I made the best of it.（私は彼女と一緒に仕事をしたくなかったが、なんとかがまんして切り抜けた）標準

No. 1066 My father is ( ) of watching soccer games on TV after dinner. 〈名古屋学院大〉
① favorite ② love ③ prefer ④ fond
Point 188 「be＋形容詞＋前置詞＋A」の形のイディオム 1066 be fond of A「Aが好きである」= like A 基本

No. 1067 You are responsible ( ) your conduct. 〈佛教大〉
① at ② for ③ with ④ on
1067 be responsible for A「Aに対して責任がある／Aが原因である」= answer for A「Aの責任を負う」(→868) 標準

No. 1068 I am ( ) his reason for going to America. 〈駒澤大〉
① ignorant of ② familiar to ③ short of ④ different from
1068 be ignorant of A「Aを知らない」標準

No. 1069 The label says this bread is ( ) of genetically modified ingredients. 〈中央大〉
① much ② free ③ good ④ characteristic
1069 be free from [of] A「Aがない」!!注意 be free from A も be free of A も「Aがない」の意味だが、たとえば「料金や税金が免除されている」の意味では be free of A の方が好まれる。標準

No. 1070 The Internet has become as ( ) as the pencil and eraser. 〈大阪経済大〉
① children familiar to ② familiar children to ③ familiar to children ④ to children familiar
1070 be familiar to A「Aによく知られている」▶本問は、be 動詞の代わりに become が用いられた become familiar to A「Aによく知られるようになる」に、原級による比較表現 as ... as ～(→179) が入り込んだ形になっている。標準

No. 1071 I am quite familiar ( ) this machine. 〈学習院大〉
① on ② to ③ up ④ with
1071 be familiar with A「Aをよく知っている」標準

No. 1072 The colleges in France are very ( ) to those in our country. 〈日本大〉
① like ② likely ③ same ④ similar
1072 be similar to A「Aに似ている」標準

No. 1073 I'm ( ) about my driving test next week. 〈芝浦工大〉
① sensational ② unknown ③ anxious ④ dreadful
1073 be sick of A「Aにうんざりしている」= be tired of A, be weary of A, be fed up with A (→1099) 標準

No. 1074 All the people in the country are anxious ( ) peace. 〈千葉商科大〉
① at ② on ③ in ④ for
1074 be anxious for A「Aを切望する」= long for A (→871), be eager for A ＋プラス be anxious about A「Aを心配している」(→1073) とあわせて押さえる。Mary was anxious about missing the last train.（メアリーは、最終電車に乗り遅れるのではないかと心配していた）標準

No. 1075 I am ( ) of today's politics. 〈中央大〉
① sick ② tire ③ boring ④ fun
1075 be sick of A「Aにうんざりしている」= be tired of A, be weary of A, be fed up with A (→1099) 標準

No. 1076 Sarah is an excellent teacher who is popular ( ) the students. 〈日本大〉
① with ② to ③ about ④ for
1076 be popular with [among] A「Aに人気がある」標準

No. 1077 The country is rich ( ) natural resources. 〈青山学院大〉
① to ② in ③ by ④ about
1077 be rich in A「Aに富んでいる／恵まれている」⇔ be poor in A「Aに乏しい」標準

No. 1078 He is not very keen ( ) classical music. 〈摂南大〉
① for ② in ③ of ④ on
1078 be keen on A「Aに熱中している」標準

No. 1079 The movie version was not ( ) to the book. 〈南山大〉
① exact ② correct ③ same ④ true
1079 be true to A「Aに忠実である」＋プラス be true of A「Aに当てはまる」(= apply to A) も頻出。(このことは学生たちに当てはまる) 標準

No. 1080 I'm ( ) of cash. May I use a credit card? 〈愛知学院大〉
① enough ② much ③ short ④ tired
1080 be short of A「Aが不足している」標準

No. 1081 He is lacking ( ) common sense. 〈姫路獨協大〉
① in ② of ③ on ④ with
1081 be lacking in A「Aを欠いている」標準

No. 1082 (a) The task is beyond his ability. (b) He is not ( ) to the task. 〈国士舘大〉
① eager ② easy ③ equal ④ even
1082 be equal to A「(人・能力などが)Aに耐えられる／匹敵する」▶(a)の beyond A's ability は「Aの力の及ばない」の意味を表す重要イディオム(→416)。標準

No. 1083 The prices are ( ) change without notice. 〈西南学院大〉
① subject to ② interested in ③ prior to ④ dependent on
1083 be subject to A「Aを受けやすい／Aに従属している」標準

No. 1084 I am not ( ) of him. 〈上智大〉
① fear ② frighten ③ afraid ④ feared
1084 be afraid of A「Aを恐れている／心配している」▶② frighten は不可。たとえば frightened あれば、be frightened of A で「Aを怖いと思う」となり可。④の fear は「…を恐れる」を意味す他動詞だから、I am not feared は「私は(他の人によって)恐れられていない」といった意味になる。基本

No. 1085 He is well ( ) of being hated by us all. 〈桜美林大〉
① known ② care ③ taken ④ aware
1085 be aware of A「Aに気づいている」= be conscious of A (→1088) 標準

No. 1086 Kazumi is entirely dependent ( ) her parents. 〈鶴見大〉
① by ② at ③ on ④ of
1086 be dependent on [upon] A「Aに頼る／Aしだいである」= depend on [upon] A (→819) ⇔ be independent of A (→791) 標準

No. 1087 My father just can't stop smoking. He should be ( ) of himself. 〈神戸松蔭女子学院大〉
① anxious ② ashamed ③ laughing ④ relaxed
1087 be ashamed of A「Aを恥じている」標準

No. 1088 My company is very ( ) of the importance of advertising. 〈東海大〉
① interested ② anxious ③ conscious ④ keen
1088 be conscious of A「Aに気づいている」= be aware of A (→1085) 標準

No. 1089 He is ( ) of his cousin's success. 〈松山大〉
① anxious ② concerned ③ jealous ④ zealous
1089 be jealous of A「Aをねたんでいる」＋プラス ほぼ同意表現の be envious of A「Aをうらやんでいる」(→p.340) も重要。標準

No. 1090 Some television programs are not suitable ( ) by children. 〈日本女子大〉
① for viewing ② in viewing ③ on seeing ④ to seeing
1090 be suitable for A「Aに適している」標準

No. 1091 I saw you talking to Mary Smith the other day. How did you become ( ) with her? 〈広島市立大〉
① acquainted ② acquainting ③ knowing ④ known
Point 189 「be＋過去分詞＋前置詞＋A」の形のイディオム 1091 be acquainted with A「Aと知り合いである／Aをよく知っている」▶本問は、be動詞の代わりに become を用いた become acquainted with A「Aと知り合いになる」の形となっている。標準

No. 1092 Mike is ( ) with a difficult problem. 〈専修大〉
① facing ② confusing ③ confronted ④ forbidden
1092 A be confronted with B「A(人)はB(困難など)に直面する」▶confront A with B「A(人)をB(困難など)に直面させる」を受身形にした表現。標準

No. 1093 Ichiro was so ( ) in the book that he didn't hear the doorbell ring. 〈駒澤大〉
① abandoned ② absorbed ③ irritated ④ obliged
1093 be absorbed in A「Aに没頭している」標準

No. 1094 He was lost ( ) thought and didn't hear me call him. 〈神田外大〉
① after ② for ③ in ④ by
1094 be lost in A「Aに夢中になる／Aに没頭している」= lose oneself in A, be absorbed in A (→1093) 標準

No. 1095 Our foreign policy is based ( ) the principle of peaceful coexistence. 〈近畿大〉
① to ② by ③ with ④ on
1095 be based on [upon] A「Aに基づいている」標準

No. 1096 She was just ( ) about your health. 〈東京薬科大〉
① afraid ② felt ③ regrettable ④ concerned
1096 be concerned about A「Aを心配する／気にする」＋プラス be concerned with A「Aに関係する／関心がある」も重要。Geography is the science that is concerned with the earth and its climate, products and inhabitants. (地理学は、地球とその気候、産物、住民を扱う科学である) 標準

No. 1097 Sheila's father ( ) her marriage to William. 〈神田外大〉
① was opposed to ② was opposite to ③ was opposite of ④ was opposed about
1097 be opposed to A「Aに反対している」＋プラス ②の be opposite to A は「Aとは正反対である」の意味を表す重要イディオム。Your views are quite opposite to mine. (あなたの見解は私のとは正反対です) 標準

No. 1098 He is well known ( ) us as the leader of the volunteer group. 〈関西学院大〉
① to ② about ③ with ④ for
1098 be known to A「A(人)によく知られている」!!注意 be known for A「Aで有名である」、be known as A「Aで通っている」との意味の違いをしっかり区別しよう。基本

No. 1099 I'm fed up with this wet weather. 〈青山学院大〉
① I'm very interested in ② I'm completely satisfied with ③ I'm indifferent to ④ I'm tired of
1099 be fed up with A「Aに飽き飽きしている」= be tired of A, be sick of A (→1075), be weary of A 標準

No. 1100 Despite ample evidence against him he was ( ) to admit that his report had not been true. 〈立教大〉
① delighted ② incapable ③ possible ④ reluctant
Point 190 「be＋形容詞[過去分詞]＋to do」の形のイディオム 1100 be reluctant to do「…することに気が進まない」= be unwilling to do ＋プラス ② incapable は to do ではなく be incapable of doing の形をとる。(→p.234 [整理 75]) 標準

No. 1101 A careless person is ( ) to make mistakes. 〈佛教大〉
① apt ② eager ③ reluctant ④ willing
1101 be apt to do「…しがちである」= tend to do, be liable to do 標準

No. 1102 If there's anything you don't understand, ( ) to ask me. 〈西南学院大〉
① feel free ② help yourself ③ get away ④ go ahead
1102 be free to do「自由に…できる」▶本問は be 動詞の代わりに feel が用いられている。標準

No. 1103 He was ( ) to get the old car. 〈駒澤大〉
① eager ② eaten ③ desired ④ empty
1103 be eager to do「…したがっている」＋プラス be eager for A「Aを切望する」も重要。標準

No. 1104 I am ( ) to know the results of the examination in chemistry. 〈武蔵大〉
① anxious ② good ③ kind ④ rude
1104 be anxious to do「…したがっている」= be eager to do (→1103) ＋プラス be anxious for A「Aを切望する」とあわせて押さえる。基本

No. 1105 You are late. You ( ) be here an hour ago. 〈東京経大〉
① have expected to ② ought to ③ should ④ were supposed to
1105 be supposed to do「…することになっている／…してください」▶be supposed to do には、(1)「…することになっている」(予定)、(2)「…しなければならない」(義務)などの用法がある。＋プラス be supposed to do は You are supposed to do の形になると「…してください」という意味になる。標準

No. 1106 Keiko was not willing to go to college until recently. 〈清泉女子大〉
① consistent ② contented ③ disappointed ④ reluctant
1106 be willing to do「…する気がある／…するのをいとわない」⇔ be reluctant to do (→1100) ▶not がつくと「…する気がしない」の意味になる。基本

No. 1107 He is bound to pass the entrance examination. 〈日本大〉
① will never ② will fortunately ③ will certainly ④ is unlikely to
1107 be bound to do「必ず…する」= be sure to do (→798) ＋プラス be bound for A「A行きである」もここで押さえておこう。The train is bound for London. (その列車はロンドン行きだ) 標準

No. 1108 "When do I have to hand in this report?" "( ), please. We have little time." 〈東京家政大〉
① Sooner or later ② Right away ③ For the moment ④ At the present
Point 191 形容詞・副詞を含むその他のイディオム 1108 right away「すぐに」= at once, right now 標準

No. 1109 We don't see her very often, but ( ) we talk with her over the telephone. 〈福岡大〉
① from times to times ② at time ③ now and then ④ in time
1109 (every) now and then [again]「ときどき」＋プラス 同意表現の from time to time (→1208), at times, on occasion, once in a while (→807) も重要。I call on Mary at times to help her with her housework. (家事を手伝うために、私はときどきメアリーを訪問します) I am not much of a movie fan, but I do go to the movies on occasion. (私はさほど映画ファンではないが、時には実際に映画に行くこともあります) 標準

No. 1110 Jim wrote to a pen pal in Japan ( ) for five years. 〈南山大〉
① off and on ② up and down ③ in and out ④ to and from
1110 off and on / on and off「断続的に／不規則に」標準

No. 1111 There are a few things that I don't like about my new job, but ( ) and large it's all right. 〈早稲田大〉
① at ② by ③ in ④ of
1111 by and large「概して／大体のところ」= as a rule (→1165), on the whole (→1195) 標準

No. 1112 I haven't earned much money as ( ). 〈拓殖大〉
① yet ② still ③ past ④ being
1112 as yet「(今までのところ)」▶as yet は通例、否定文で用いる。＋プラス 同意表現の so far「今まで」(= until [till] now) (→1116) も重要。標準

No. 1113 I was busy with my homework last night. I didn't have time to eat supper, ( ) watch TV. 〈名城大〉
① as to ② but for ③ except for ④ let alone
1113 let alone A「Aは言うまでもなく」▶let alone A は通例、否定文の後で用い、Aには名詞や動詞が来る点を押さえておく。標準
No.1114 Salter held the bag by the corners and shook it ( ). ① down upside ② inside up ③ up inside ④ upside down 〈駒大〉
1114 upside down 「逆さまに」

No.1115 The rescue team tried to save the drowning man in vain. ① with courage ② without success ③ with skill ④ without haste 〈東海大〉
1115 in vain 「（努力の）甲斐なく／無駄に」 = vainly, for nothing (→ 1152), to no purpose

No.1116 This is the most beautiful place I have visited so far. ① no where ② distant ③ till now ④ not near 〈流通経済大〉
1116 so far 「今まで」 = until [till] now

No.1117 Jane was badly off before she came to Japan. ① lacking in ability ② short of money ③ in a bad temper ④ in trouble 〈立命館大〉
1117 be badly [poorly] off 「暮らし向きが悪い」
+プラス 反意表現の be well off 「暮らし向きがよい」も頻出。
His parents are well off; they have bought him a new car for his birthday. (彼の両親は裕福で、誕生日に彼に新車を買ってやった)

No.1118 What with the smoke and the noise, the party made me feel quite ill. ① By means of ② In spite of ③ Instead of ④ Because of 〈立命館大〉
1118 what with A and (what with) B 「AやらBやらで」
▶通例、よくない理由を2つ以上あげる場合に用いる。この場合の what は副詞で「いくぶん／ある程度」の意味。

No.1119 This computer is more or less what I want. ① nevertheless ② incidentally ③ roughly ④ precisely 〈大阪学院大〉
1119 more or less 「多かれ少なかれ／ほとんど／およそ」
+プラス 類似形の sooner or later 「遅かれ早かれ」も頻出。
He will come sooner or later. (彼は、遅かれ早かれやって来るだろう)

No.1120 More often than not he loses his temper. ① Once in a while ② Very rarely ③ More than usual ④ Most of the time 〈立命館大〉
1120 more often than not 「しばしば／たいてい」
▶ ④ most of the time は「たいてい」の意味を表すイディオム。

No.1121 It is next to impossible for me to help him out at the moment. ① absolutely ② almost ③ partly ④ perhaps 〈愛知学院大〉
1121 next to A 「ほとんどA」 = almost A
!!注意 next to A の A には通例、否定の意味の形容詞、または nothing などが来る。

No.1122 Mary told him once and for all that she wouldn't go out with him. ① all at once ② many times ③ in the first place ④ in a final manner 〈千葉工大〉
1122 once (and) for all 「これを最後に／きっぱりと」
▶ ① all at once は「突然に」(→ 1182)、③ in the first place は「まず第一に」の意味を表すイディオム。

Point 192 2語からなる名詞を含むイディオム 1123～1132
No.1123 He is ( ) nature a wise, kind man. ① by ② for ③ to ④ with 〈青山学院大〉
1123 by nature 「生来／生まれながら」

No.1124 If you want to know anything ( ) detail, feel free to email me. ① along ② at ③ in ④ off 〈東京理科大〉
1124 in detail 「詳細に」

No.1125 No one knows ( ) if there is life on other planets. ① certain ② for certain ③ better ④ to be sure 〈拓殖大〉
1125 for certain 「はっきりと／確かに」 = for sure

No.1126 Mr. Patterson arrived ( ) time, not a minute early or a minute late. ① at ② for ③ in ④ on 〈東北学院大〉
1126 on time 「時間どおりに」 = punctually

No.1127 Tom will be able to arrive ( ) for the ceremony. ① in time ② off limit ③ time off ④ time slip 〈武庫川女子大〉
1127 in time (for A) 「(Aに)間に合って」
+プラス in time には「やがて」の意味もある。また behind time 「遅れて」もここでおさえる。

No.1128 I didn't like the book at first, but ( ) degrees I got to enjoy reading it. ① by ② in ③ on ④ with 〈成城大〉
1128 by degrees 「徐々に／次第に」 = gradually
▶ get to do 「～するようになる」

No.1129 I would like to speak to you ( ) private. ① at ② in ③ of ④ to 〈学習院大〉
1129 in private 「内密に／ひそかに」 ⇔ in public 「人前で／公然と」

No.1130 Mr. Takizawa and Mr. Higashi are ( ) work now. ① on ② at ③ from ④ by 〈産能大〉
1130 at work 「仕事中で」
+プラス 類似表現の at table 「食事中で」、at rest 「休憩中で」、at play 「遊んでいて」も押さえる。

No.1131 Instead of sending somebody on your behalf, you had better go and speak in ( ). ① change ② line ③ person ④ yourself 〈武蔵大〉
1131 in person 「自分で／本人自らが」
▶ on [in] A's behalf 「Aの代理として」 = on [in] behalf of A (→ 1239)。

No.1132 You should take an umbrella with you just ( ) case. ① at ② of ③ as ④ in 〈名城大〉
1132 (just) in case 「(通例、文尾で)万一の場合に備えて」
+プラス in case は接続詞としてもよく使われる (→ 374)。

No.1133 The policeman was ( ) that night. ① on purpose ② in advance ③ by accident ④ on duty 〈近畿大〉
1133 on duty 「勤務時間中で／当番で」 ⇔ off duty 「勤務時間外で／非番で」
+プラス on purpose 「故意に」(→ 1153)、in advance 「あらかじめ」(→ 1149)、by accident 「偶然に」(→ 1150)。

No.1134 The escaped prisoners are still ( ) in the area. ① at stake ② at large ③ at random ④ at any cost 〈青山学院大〉
1134 at large 「捕まらないで」
+プラス at large には、名詞の後で「一般の／全体としての」の意味を表す用法もある。
That can be said of mankind at large. (そのことは人間全般について言える)

No.1135 When he writes, he always keeps a dictionary ( ). ① at hand ② from hand ③ for hand ④ with hand 〈日本大〉
1135 at hand 「手元に」
+プラス at hand には「(時間的に)近づいて」の意味もある。この場合、直前に close や near が用いられることが多い。
The festival is near [close] at hand. (その祭りはもうすぐだ)

No.1136 At the beginning of each term I always tell some jokes to make the newcomers feel ( ). ① at ② for ③ of ④ with 〈関西学院大〉
1136 at ease 「気楽に／くつろいで」
▶ ④ with を入れた with ease は「容易に」の意。「with + 抽象名詞」=副詞の用法例(→ 405)。

No.1137 Three sites are ( ) consideration for the new factory. ① above ② of ③ under ④ with 〈愛知医科大〉
1137 under consideration 「考慮中で／検討中で」
+プラス 類似表現の under discussion 「討議中で」、under repair 「修理中で」、under construction 「工事中で」も押さえる。

No.1138 We'll soon have to tackle the problem ( ) earnest. ① in ② at ③ for ④ on 〈立命館大〉
1138 in earnest 「まじめに／本気で」

No.1139 They have nothing at all ( ) common. ① on ② with ③ for ④ in 〈中央大〉
1139 in common 「共通の／共通に」

No.1140 I found it elegant furniture, but it was not ( ) sale. ① for ② with ③ all ④ others 〈中京大〉
1140 for sale 「売り物の」
+プラス on sale 「販売されて」も一緒に覚えておこう。
Concert tickets are on sale at this office. (コンサートのチケットは当所で販売中です)

No.1141 I used to live in Sydney, but ( ) present I'm living in Tokyo. ① for ② on ③ at ④ in 〈上智大〉
1141 at present 「現在は」

No.1142 Children need many things, but, above all, they need love. ① voluntarily ② especially ③ far from ④ on earth 〈亜細亜大〉
1142 above all 「とりわけ」 = especially

No.1143 He will get here before long. ① soon ② late ③ later ④ early 〈日本医大〉
1143 before long 「まもなく」 = soon

No.1144 That American student is quite at home in Japanese politics. ① well off in ② elastic in ③ knowledgeable about ④ easy with 〈関西外大〉
1144 (be) at home (in[with] A) 「(Aに)精通している」

No.1145 Penny feels at home with Roger's family. ① regular ② at heart ③ on edge ④ comfortable 〈亜細亜大〉
1145 at home 「くつろいで／気楽な」 = comfortable
+プラス at home は、前問および本問の意味以外に、①「祖国で」、②「在宅して」の意味でも用いられる。

No.1146 He sat there for hours on end. ① silently ② continuously ③ at last ④ strait 〈名古屋外大〉
1146 on end 「続けて」 = continuously

No.1147 The project is not yet under way. ① closed down ② set about ③ in progress ④ half over 〈日本大〉
1147 under way 「進行中で」 = in progress

No.1148 You must return my money next Friday without fail. ① for certain ② partly ③ eventually ④ thoroughly 〈亜細亜大〉
1148 without fail 「必ず／きっと」 = for certain (→ 1125), for sure

No.1149 They knew about it in advance. ① at most ② beforehand ③ for certain ④ least of all 〈中部大〉
1149 in advance 「あらかじめ／前もって」 = beforehand

No.1150 I met her sister on the campus by chance. ① unwillingly ② fortunately ③ reasonably ④ accidentally 〈札幌学院大〉
1150 by chance 「偶然に」 = accidentally, by accident

No.1151 At length the two countries reached an agreement after much discussion. ① Strongly ② Before long ③ At last ④ Easily 〈亜細亜大〉
1151 at length 「ついに／ようやく／やっと」 = at last

No.1152 All my efforts were for nothing. ① unlikely ② in vain ③ unhappily ④ for granted 〈近畿大〉
1152 for nothing 「むだに」 = in vain (→ 1115), to no purpose
+プラス for nothing では、これ以外に「①無料で(→ 265)、②何の理由もなく」の意味も押さえる。
① She got it for nothing. (彼女はそれをただで手に入れた)
② They quarreled for nothing. (彼らは何の理由もなくけんかした)

No.1153 I think she did it on purpose. ① accidentally ② intentionally ③ reluctantly ④ willingly 〈帝京大〉
1153 on purpose 「故意に／わざと」 = intentionally, deliberately

No.1154 In short they had a difficult trip. ① At least ② For a while ③ For instance ④ To sum up 〈愛知工大〉
1154 in short 「要するに／手短に言えば」 = in brief, to sum up
▶ ① at least 「少なくとも」、② for a while 「しばらくの間」

No.1155 The two students told their teacher about the strange experience by turns. ① persuasively ② alternately ③ repeatedly ④ expressively 〈愛知工大〉
1155 by turns 「交替で／かわるがわる」 = alternately

No.1156 Has Jack left the office for good this time? ① excellently ② truly ③ permanently ④ willingly 〈札幌学院大〉
1156 for good (and all) 「永久に／これを最後に」 = permanently, forever

No.1157 Yesterday I cut my finger by mistake. ① willingly ② deeply ③ accidentally ④ intentionally 〈明海大〉
1157 by mistake 「誤って／間違って」
▶ accidentally の本来の意味は「偶然に(=by chance)」であるが、英作文の内容によっては、本問のように「誤って(=by mistake)」の意味で用いることもある。
I accidentally fell down the stairs. (誤って階段からころげ落ちた)

Point 193 3語からなる名詞を含むイディオム
No.1158 We mustn't speak ill of a man ( ) his back. ① over ② after ③ behind ④ under 〈名古屋学院大〉
1158 behind A's back 「Aのいないところで」 ⇔ to A's face 「Aに面と向かって」
+プラス 文中の speak ill of A 「Aの悪口を言う」も重要イディオム(→ 789)。

No.1159 In the judo match, he threw his opponent ( ) no time at all. ① at ② in ③ on ④ to 〈立命館大〉
1159 in no time 「すぐに／間もなく」

No.1160 He thinks that life is a voyage in a ( ). ① score ② sense ③ extent ④ extension 〈駒澤大〉
1160 in a sense 「ある意味では」 = in a way

No.1161 I can express myself in English ( ), but I still have a lot to learn. ① as much as possible ② by all means ③ to some extent ④ for the moment 〈名城大〉
1161 to some extent 「ある程度」
+プラス to a great [large] extent なら「大いに」の意味になる。

No.1162 She refused to do what they wanted. ( ), she wasn't going to let them push her around. ① Overall ② By the way ③ In other words ④ In all 〈関西外大〉
1162 in other words 「言いかえれば」 = to put it another way, that is to say

No.1163 I glance through the newspapers and watch TV every day so as not to be ( ) the times. ① up ② behind ③ late ④ slow 〈立命館大〉
1163 behind the times 「時代遅れで／時勢に遅れて」
+プラス behind time は「遅れて」の意味。

No.1164 I would like to withdraw comment on that for the present. ① right away ② to the moment ③ now and then ④ for the time being 〈東京理科大〉
1164 for the present 「さしあたり／当分は」 = for the time being (→ 1197), for some time
▶ ③ now and then 「時々」も押さえておこう(→ 1109)。

No.1165 Most students finish their coursework by the end of May as a ( ). ① majority ② reality ③ rule ④ fact 〈西南学院大〉
1165 as a rule 「概して／大体のところ」 = on the whole (→ 1195), generally, by and large (→ 1111)

No.1166 We were at a ( ) where to go. ① cross ② loss ③ road ④ crossroad 〈拓殖大〉
1166 (be) at a loss 「途方にくれる」
+プラス (be) at a loss for words なら「言葉につまる」の意味。

No.1167 I'd like to see the merchandise ( ). ① at first hand ② at a first hand ③ at the first hand ④ at first hands 〈学習院女子大〉
1167 at first hand 「直接に／じかに」
+プラス at second hand 「間接に」もここで押さえる。

No.1168 Children are likely to get ( ) if no one cares about disciplining them. ① away from the hand ② away from hand ③ out of hand ④ out of the hand 〈東海大〉
1168 out of hand 「手に負えないで」
+プラス out of hand には「即座に(=immediately)」の意味もある。

No.1169 "Could you tell me where the elevator is?" "I'm sorry, but it's out of ( )." ① energy ② hand ③ order ④ place 〈センター試験〉
1169 out of order 「故障して」 ⇔ in order 「順調で／きちんとして」
!!注意 out of order は、原則として公共の施設や機械の場合に用いる。
+プラス ④ out of place 「場違いな／不適当な」も押さえておこう。

No.1170 (a) This type of shoe is no longer in fashion. (b) This type of shoe is out of ( ). ① date ② order ③ leather ④ shine 〈関西学院大〉
1170 out of date 「時代遅れで」 ⇔ up to date 「最新の」
+プラス out of fashion 「すたれて」 ⇔ in fashion 「流行して」も重要イディオム。

No.1171 Your explanation was very much to the ( ). ① dot ② place ③ point ④ spot 〈千葉商大〉
1171 to the point 「要領を得た」 ⇔ beside [off] the point 「要点をはずれて／要領を得ない」(→ 1193)

No.1173 Students travel half-price on that airline. ( ), have you bought your ticket for New York yet? ① As a result ② By the way ③ Nevertheless ④ What is more 〈京都産大〉
1173 by the way 「ところで」
▶ ① as a result 「結果として」、④ what is more 「その上に／さらに」(→ 309)

No.1174 Take a camera ( )—there will be a chance of some unforgettable shots during the trip. ① by all means ② by any chance ③ by chance ④ by no means 〈東京電機大〉
1174 by all means 「ぜひとも」
▶ ② by any chance 「ひょっとして」(→ 1184)、④ by no means 「決して...でない」(→ 484)。 p. 175 [整理 45] も参照。

No.1175 That picture doesn't seem ugly to me; ( ), I think it's beautiful. ① however ② in opposition ③ on the contrary ④ on the other hand 〈センター試験〉

No.1176 He went to see the football game in spite of his doctor's advice ( ) the contrary. ① in ② on ③ at ④ to 〈慶應義塾大〉
1176 to the contrary 「(修飾する語句の後で)それと反対の[に]」

No.1177 Keep all medicines out of ( ) of our baby. ① touch ② hand ③ reach ④ area 〈福岡国際大〉

+プラス out of [beyond] A's reach 「(Aの)手の届かないところに」 ⇔ within (A's) reach 「(Aの)手の届くところに」の関係をしっかり理解しよう。

No. 1188 I don't let anything get in my way. I keep trying.

⇔ out of A's way 「Aのじゃまにならないように」
get in A's way 「Aのじゃまをする」の意味になる。
＋プラス in the way (of A) 「（Aの）じゃまになって」⇔ out of the way (of A) 「（Aの）じゃまにならないように」という表現も押さえておこう。

No. 1208 We would like to have barbecue parties from time to time.

= occasionally
＋プラス 「ときどき」の意味を表すイディオムは、本問の他に、at times (→ 1109), on occasion (→ 1109), once in a while (→ 807), (every) now and then [again] (→ 1109) の4つを押さえる。

No. 1210 His grandmother was kind enough to make good on his debts.

＋プラス make good (on) a loss 「損失を補てんする」も押さえる。

＋プラス up in the air には副詞句「空高く」の意味もあるので注意。

No. 1212 The train was delayed ( ) the heavy rain.

Point 195 理由を表す群前置詞
以下の群前置詞はほぼ同意の表現と考えてよい。
1212 on account of A 「Aの理由で」
▶③ for the sake of A 「Aの（利益の）ために／Aを目的として」（→ 1218）

No. 1213 Severe food shortages will occur, ( ) to the effects of global warming.

1213 owing to A 「Aの理由で」

No. 1214 The airport was closed ( ) the fog.
① because ② by way of ③ for all ④ due to 〈亜細亜大〉
1214 due to A 「Aの理由で」
＋プラス ⑦ be due to A 「Aが原因［理由］である」, ⑨ be due to do 「…する予定である」の用法も押さえる。
⑦ Her absence was due to illness.
（彼女の欠席は病気によるものだった）
⑨ She is due to come here today.
（今日，彼女はここに来る予定だ）

No. 1215 ( ) your kind cooperation, we were able to finish the project within three days.

1215 thanks to A 「Aの理由で／Aのおかげで」
!!注意 Aには良いことだけでなく、悪いことも来ることに注意。
Thanks to the terrible weather, we had to postpone our trip.
（ひどい天気だったので，私たちは旅行を延期しなければならなかった）

No. 1216 The competition to get into that company was very high. Nonetheless, she was successful ( ) of her clear motivation.

▶② by way of A 「Aのつもりで／Aを経由して」（→ 1237）, ③ in favor of A 「Aを支持して／Aに賛成して」（→ 1233）, ④ in place of A 「Aの代わりに」（→ 1240）, = instead of A

▶① の against は「…に反対して」の意味があるが，主語の she が「反対の姿勢」を持っているわけではないので，本問では不可。

No. 1222 I cannot agree with her ( ) regards this.

No. 1223 As ( ) me, I don't mind working on the holiday.

1223 as for A 「（文頭で）Aについて言えば」

He has no friend to talk with other than Ted.

⇔ against A (→ 401)

No. 1234 Living in New York is cheap in ( ) with living in Tokyo.
① compare ② comparison ③ compared ④ comparing 〈拓殖大〉
1234 in [by] comparison with A 「Aと比較すると」

No. 1235 To tell you the truth, I don't like Tom very much. He considers everything ( ) profit and loss.
① thanks to ② at the cost of ③ in terms of ④ for lack of 〈東邦大〉
1235 in terms of A 「Aの点から」
▶① thanks to A 「Aの理由で」（→ 1215）, ② at the cost of A 「Aを犠牲にして」（→ 1243）, ④ for lack of A 「Aの不足のために」（→ 1230）

No. 1236 Politics in Japan is getting complicated. What do you think ( ) regard to this problem?
① at ② in ③ for ④ by 〈神戸松蔭女子学院大〉
1236 in regard to A 「Aに関して」
= in respect of A

No. 1237 He returned home ( ) New York.
① in honor of ② by way of ③ for the purpose of ④ in case of 〈愛知工大〉
1237 by way of A 「Aを経由して」
＋プラス by way of A は「Aのつもりで」の意味でも用いられる。
She said that by way of a joke.
（彼女は冗談のつもりでそう言った）

No. 1238 Who is in ( ) of the office while the boss is away?
① charge ② responsibility ③ care ④ head 〈立命館大〉
1238 in charge of A 「Aの担当で／Aの責任を負っている」
▶本問のように，be 動詞の後で補語的に使われることが多い。

No. 1239 The secretary spoke ( ) of the minister, who was ill.
① because ② in consequence ③ in spite ④ on behalf 〈中部大〉
1239 on [in] behalf of A 「Aの代理として／代表として」
＋プラス on [in] behalf of A は「Aのために」の意味でも用いられる。
They work on behalf of the country.
（彼らは国のために働く）

No. 1240 For this recipe you can always use olive oil in ( ) of butter.
① regard ② manner ③ place ④ charge 〈北海学園大〉
1240 in place of A 「Aの代わりに」
= instead of A
▶④ in charge of A は「Aの担当で／Aの責任を負っている」の意味（→ 1238）。

No. 1241 He explained the strange phenomena ( ) recent scientific knowledge.
① in the light of ② in case of ③ in point of ④ in respect of 〈久留米大〉
Point 200 4語からなる群前置詞
1241 in (the) light of A 「Aの観点から／Aを考慮して」

No. 1242 ( ) the sight of a snake, the girl gave a cry.
① On ② With ③ To ④ At 〈桜美林大〉
1242 at the sight of A 「Aを見ると」

No. 1243 He argues that the tax cut will benefit the rich at the ( ) of the poor.
① expense ② help ③ mercy ④ suspense 〈学習院大〉
1243 at the expense [cost] of A 「Aを犠牲にして」

No. 1244 We spent the night on the mountain ( ) the wind and rain.
① at the sight of ② at the cost of ③ at the mercy of ④ at the rate of 〈青山学院大〉
1244 at the mercy of A 「Aのなすがままに」
No. 1365 I was caught in a traffic ( ) yesterday. ① jam ② junction ③ pack ④ tightness 〈浜松大〉
1365 a traffic jam 「交通渋滞」
▶jamは「込み合い/雑踏」の意味で、「交通渋滞」は a traffic jam である。[基本]
▶be caught in Aは「A(雨や交通渋滞など)にあう」(→38)。

No. 1366 Her jokes about the Japanese were in very poor ( ). ① humor ② view ③ feeling ④ taste 〈獨協大〉
1366 in poor [bad] taste 「下品で」
▶tasteには「品/センス」の意味もある。[標準]
＋プラス 反意表現の in good taste 「上品で」もここで押さえておこう。

No. 1367 It's a ( ) your wife couldn't come. I really wanted to meet her. ① harm ② shame ③ sorrow ④ trouble 〈センター試験〉
1367 It is a shame+that 節 「…は残念なことだ」[発展]
▶shameは「恥ずかしさ」の他にも a shame で「残念なこと/遺憾なこと」(=a pity)を表す。本問のように It is a shame+that 節の形で用いられることも多い。なお、本問では接続詞 that が省略されている。
▶③ sorrow「悲しみ」は、親しい人の不幸などの不幸なことへの悲しみを表す場合に用いる。また、本問のような形式主語の構文で用いることはない。

No. 1368 The cutting down of trees for firewood is an example of unwise land use ( ). ① drills ② exercises ③ practices ④ trials 〈上智大〉
1368 practice 「社会的習慣/社会の習わし」[標準]
＋プラス 「個人的な習慣」は habit を用いる。(→718)

No. 1369 When you fill out the application, be sure to state all your job ( ). ① qualifications ② qualifies ③ qualifying ④ qualitative 〈北里大〉
1369 qualification 「資格/適性」[標準]

No. 1370 A man is known by the ( ) he keeps. ① company ② corporation ③ friend ④ group 〈千葉商科大〉
1370 A man is known by the company he keeps. 「人は付き合っている仲間でわかる」[標準]
▶company には、単数形と複数形が同じ形の集合名詞で「仲間/友だち」の意味を表す用法がある。the company he keeps は「付き合っている仲間たち」の意味。本問は「ことわざ」なので、そのまま覚えておこう。

No. 1371 The show will be on the ( ) within a week. ① air ② television ③ ticket ④ wire 〈清泉女子大〉
1371 on (the) air 「放送されて」[標準]
▶air には (the) air で「テレビ[ラジオ]による放送」の意味を表す用法がある。on (the) air 「放送されて」で覚えておこう。
＋プラス 反意表現の off the air 「放送していないで」も重要。

No. 1372 A ( ) is a down and up movement of the head used in many countries to show that you agree with or understand something. ① nod ② pat ③ shake ④ wink 〈センター試験〉
1372 nod 「(同意を表す)うなずき」[標準]
▶② pat 「(軽く)たたくこと」、③ shake 「振ること」、④ wink 「目くばせ」

No. 1373 The other day we gained ( ) to the governor. ① access ② appointment ③ interview ④ meet 〈東北学院大〉
1373 access to A 「Aとの面会(許可)」[標準]
▶名詞の access 「近づくこと/接近」は gain[obtain/get] access to A で「Aに面会[接近/参入]する」の意味を表す。

No. 1374 Rapid weight loss can be a ( ) of a serious illness. ① consciousness ② involvement ③ sign ④ doubt 〈芝浦工大〉
1374 sign 「兆候/表れ」[標準]
▶① consciousness 「意識」、② involvement 「関与」

No. 1375 The department store has been losing more and more ( ) because of this bad economy. ① patients ② customers ③ passengers ④ audience 〈札幌学院大〉
1375 customer 「お店の客/顧客」[標準]
▶① patient 「患者」、④ audience 「聴衆」

No. 1376 We had to get ( ) to erect an antenna in front of the main entrance. ① admission ② application ③ permission ④ prescription 〈南山大〉
1376 permission to do 「…する許可」[標準]
▶① admission 「入場[入会/入社/入学]許可」、② application 「申請/要請」、④ prescription 「(病気の)処方せん/指示」

No. 1377 As the ( ) of living is higher in Tokyo than in Nagoya, I decided to live in Nagoya. ① expensive ② money ③ price ④ cost 〈南山大〉
1377 the cost of living 「生活費」[標準]
▶名詞の cost 「費用/経費」を用いた the cost of living は「生活費」の意味を表す。(→p.257[整理86])

No. 1378 We gave the singer a big ( ). ① hand ② leg ③ nose ④ stomach 〈国士舘大〉
1378 a big[good] hand 「大きな拍手」[標準]
▶名詞の hand には「拍手」の意味がある。give A a big[good] hand で「Aに大きな拍手を送る」の意味を表す。

No. 1379 Brett has many spare-time ( ): he swims, paints, plays the violin, and so on. ① actions ② exercises ③ activities ④ habits 〈センター試験〉
1379 activity 「(反復される一定の)活動」[標準]
▶① action 「行動/行為」、② exercise 「運動」、④ habit 「習慣/癖」

No. 1380 My grandmother always said you should sweat to reduce the ( ) when you have the flu. ① medicine ② illness ③ fever ④ pressure 〈センター試験〉
1380 fever 「病気による熱/発熱」[標準]
▶① medicine 「薬」、② illness 「病気」、④ pressure 「圧力」

No. 1381 When the rich man passed away, he left a large ( ) to a good cause. ① cash ② wealth ③ money ④ fortune 〈南山大〉
1381 a large fortune 「大きな財産」[標準]
▶fortune には「幸運」の他に「財産」の意味がある。
▶① cash は不可算名詞で「現金」の意味(→p.257[整理86])。② wealth も「富/財産」の意味があるが、wealth は通例、不可算名詞。large wealth とは言わない。great wealth 「莫大な財産」は可。

No. 1382 My TV set is almost 15 years old, but it still has a good ( ). ① message ② photo ③ picture ④ scene 〈センター試験〉
1382 picture 「(テレビ・映画の)画面/画質」[標準]
▶① message 「伝言」、② photo 「写真」、④ scene 「場面」

No. 1383 "May I speak to Mr. Hall, please?" "I'm sorry, he's not here at the moment. Can I take a ( )?" ① memo ② message ③ note ④ record 〈センター試験〉
1383 take a message 「伝言をうかがう」[標準]
▶take a message で「伝言をうかがう」の意味(→1265)。
▶① memo 「簡単な記録」=memorandum、③ note 「覚え書き」、④ record 「記録」

No. 1384 His shoes were so old that his ( ) were sticking out of them. ① tips ② toes ③ thumbs ④ fingers 〈駿河台大〉
1384 toe 「つま先/足の指」[標準]
▶① tip 「先端」、③ thumb 「手の親指」、④ finger 「手の指」
＋プラス 「足の親指」は big[large] toe ということも押さえておこう。

No. 1385 Getting used to a foreign culture is a ( ) that takes some time. ① career ② characteristic ③ policy ④ process 〈センター試験〉
1385 process 「過程」[標準]
▶① career 「経歴」、② characteristic 「特徴」、③ policy 「方針」

No. 1386 When you buy something that costs \985, and you pay with a \1,000 bill, how much ( ) should the store give you back? ① rate ② exchange ③ change ④ trade 〈東京経大〉
1386 change 「つり銭/小銭」[標準]
▶名詞の change には、「変化」の他にも「つり銭/小銭」の意味がある(→732 ＋プラス 1279)。
▶① rate 「割合/相場」、② exchange 「為替」、④ trade 「商売/貿易」

No. 1387 A ( ) is someone who has been hurt or killed in an accident or during a crime. ① patient ② rival ③ surgeon ④ victim 〈センター試験〉
1387 victim 「犠牲者」[標準]
▶① patient 「患者」(→p.259[整理87])、② rival 「競争相手」、③ surgeon 「外科医」

No. 1388 Because of improved technology, factory ( ) is expected to rise this year. ① outbreak ② outcome ③ outlook ④ output 〈学習院大〉
1388 output 「生産高」[標準]
▶① outbreak 「発生」、② outcome 「成果」、③ outlook 「展望」

No. 1389 Since people use air conditioners a lot in summer, electricity ( ) rises sharply. ① consumption ② quantity ③ amount ④ sum 〈南山大〉
1389 consumption 「消費量」[標準]

No. 1390 Kyoto is a ( ) for tourists. ① must ② service ③ hole ④ look 〈國學院大〉
1390 a must 「必見のもの」[発展]
▶must には名詞用法があり、「必見[必読/必修]のもの/不可欠なもの」の意味を表す。

No. 1391 The view from the ( ) of the mountain was extremely beautiful. ① altitude ② valley ③ hill ④ summit 〈立教大〉
1391 summit 「(山の)頂上」[標準]
▶① altitude 「高度/標高」、② valley 「谷間」、③ hill 「丘/小山」

No. 1392 A ( ) is an area of land without trees or water, usually covered with sand. ① hill ② desert ③ valley ④ mountain 〈名古屋学院大〉
1392 desert 「砂漠」[標準]
▶① hill 「丘/小山」、③ valley 「谷間」、④ mountain 「山」

No. 1393 Agricultural ( ) sprayed on crops do great harm to both human beings and animals. ① medicines ② drugs ③ chemicals ④ harvests 〈南山大〉
1393 agricultural chemicals 「農薬」[発展]
▶形容詞の chemical は「化学の」の意味だが、名詞の chemical は通例、複数形で「化学薬品[製品]」の意味を表す。

No. 1394 I had to take a ( ) off on that day because of a severe headache. ① day ② holiday ③ rest ④ work 〈桜美林大〉
1394 take a day off 「1日休みをとる」[標準]
!!注意 take a day off, take a holiday 「休暇をとる」、take a rest 「ひと休みする」をまとめて覚えておこう。

No. 1395 I'd like to send this large package to New Zealand by registered ( ). ① letter ② mail ③ post office ④ stamps 〈学習院大〉
1395 by registered mail 「書留郵便で」[標準]
▶mail には「郵便(制度)」の意味があり、by mail で「郵便で」の意味を表す。
▶registered は形容詞で「書留の/登録された」の意味。
!!注意 イギリス英語では、一般的に by mail よりも by post を用いる。

No. 1396 If a cube has sides ten centimeters long, its ( ) is 1,000 cubic centimeters. ① area ② length ③ volume ④ width 〈摂南大〉
1396 volume 「体積」[標準]
▶cube は「立方体」の意味。① area 「面積」、② length 「長さ」、④ width 「幅/広さ」

No. 1397 The yen is the ( ) of currency used in Japan. ① unit ② union ③ unity ④ united 〈杏林大〉
1397 unit 「(計量の)単位」[標準]
▶② union 「結合/組合/連合」、③ unity 「単一(性)/調和」、④ united 「団結した」

No. 1398 It's clear there's a strong ( ) between smoking and heart disease. ① effect ② joint ③ link ④ sense 〈南山大〉
1398 a strong link between A and B 「AとBの強い関連」[標準]
▶名詞の link には「関連/つながり」の意味があり、a link between A and B で「AとBの関連」の意味を表す。

No. 1399 Sometimes, it takes a long time to reach technical support on the phone. From the customer's ( ), it has to run smoothly. ① perspective ② permission ③ persuasion ④ percussion 〈芝浦工大〉
1399 from A's perspective / from the perspective of A 「A(人)の観点から」[標準]

No. 1400 Penelope put so much salt in the soup that she spoiled the ( ). ① flavor ② scent ③ smell ④ odor 〈関東学院大〉
1400 flavor 「(ある物に特有の)風味/味」[発展]
▶② scent 「(特に)好ましい香り/香り」、③ smell 「におい/悪臭」、④ odor 「(物から出る)におい/臭気」

No. 1401 My mother is making a fast ( ) after the operation on her knee last week. ① repair ② treatment ③ recovery ④ benefit 〈センター試験〉
1401 recovery 「回復」[標準]
▶① repair 「修理」、② treatment 「治療」、④ benefit 「利益」

No. 1402 Jack's major is ( ); he often speaks excitedly to us about how the mind works and influences behavior. ① geography ② chemistry ③ psychology ④ geometry 〈京都外大〉
1402 psychology 「心理学」[標準]
▶① geography 「地理(学)」、② chemistry 「化学」、④ geometry 「幾何(学)」

No. 1403 ( ) is the scientific study of forces such as heat, light, and sound, and the way they affect objects. ① Politics ② Chemistry ③ Physics ④ Geography 〈センター試験〉
1403 physics 「物理学」[標準]
▶① politics 「政治(学)」、② chemistry 「化学」、④ geography 「地理(学)」

No. 1404 I'd like to have some rather ( ) coffee now. ① deep ② dense ③ strong ④ thick 〈慶應義塾大〉
1404 strong coffee [tea] 「濃いコーヒー [お茶]」[標準]
▶strong には「(コーヒー・お茶が)濃い」の意味がある。
＋プラス 「(色が)濃い」は ① deep、「(霧が)濃い」は ② dense や ④ thick、「(スープが)濃い」は ④ thick を、それぞれ用いる。deep blue 「濃い青」、dense[thick] fog 「濃霧」、thick soup 「濃いスープ」で覚えておこう。

No. 1405 Ruth didn't like the steak because it was too ( ). ① tough ② strong ③ hard ④ solid 〈学習院大〉
1405 The steak is too tough. 「そのステーキはかたすぎる」[標準]
▶tough には「頑丈な/強硬な」などの他に「(ステーキなどが)かたい/かみにくい」の意味がある。
▶③ hard にも「かたい」の意味があるが、hard steak とは言わない。「かたくてかみ切れないもの」には tough を用いることに注意。

No. 1406 The portions at this restaurant are ( ), so I don't know if I can eat all of mine. ① delicious ② dominant ③ generous ④ grateful 〈立命館大〉
1406 generous 「たっぷりの」[標準]

No. 1407 Some schools have very ( ) rules of behavior which must be obeyed. ① strong ② solid ③ straight ④ strict 〈東海大〉
1407 strict rules 「厳しい規則」[標準]
▶「(規則・命令などが)厳しい」の意味では strict を用いる。

No. 1408 The traffic was so ( ) that we couldn't be in time for the train. ① great ② large ③ big ④ heavy 〈法政大〉
1408 heavy traffic 「激しい交通量」[基本]
▶heavy には「(交通量が)激しい」の意味がある。
＋プラス 「(交通量が)少ない」場合には light を用いることも押さえておこう。

No. 1409 Close your eyes and take a ( ) breath to relax. ① deep ② heavy ③ short ④ thick 〈中部大〉
1409 take a deep breath 「深呼吸をする」[標準]
▶deep は「(呼吸・ため息などが)深い」の場合にも用いられる。

No. 1410 Every winter, colds are ( ) at school. ① familiar ② popular ③ broad ④ common 〈センター試験〉
1410 Colds are common. 「風邪がはやる」
▶common には「ありふれた/ありがちな」の意味がある。
▶① familiar にも「ありふれた」の意味があるが、a familiar legend 「ありふれた伝説」のように「よく知られている」の意味。② popular にも「はやって」の意味があるが、a popular song 「流行歌」のように「流行している/人気のある」の意味。③ broad には「広範囲に及ぶ」の意味があるが、broad support 「幅広い支持」のように支持や合意(agreement)などの名詞を修飾する。この意味では、通例、限定用法(名詞を修飾)で用いる。

No. 1411 "Is this the way to the station?" "Yes, that's the ( ) way." ① good ② right ③ true ④ well 〈センター試験〉
1411 the right A 「適切なA/正しいA」
▶right には the right A の形で「適切なA/正しいA」の意味を表す用法がある。A には、way の他にも time, place, number, train, direction, person などがくる。
＋プラス 反意表現の the wrong A 「間違ったA」も重要(→681)。

No. 1412 This is a ( ) leather jacket, not an imitation. ① honest ② strict ③ genuine ④ realistic 〈清泉女子大〉
1412 genuine leather 「本物の革」
▶genuine には「本物の」の意味がある。

No. 1413 "How beautiful your diamond ring is!" "This diamond is not ( ), I'm afraid." ① right ② correct ③ real ④ true 〈鹿児島国際大〉
1413 real 「本物の」
▶real には genuine と同様に「本物の」の意味がある。

No. 1414 My watch is always four or five minutes ( ). ① early ② fast ③ quick ④ soon 〈福岡歯科大〉
1414 My watch is five minutes fast. 「私の腕時計は5分進んでいる」
▶fast には「(時計が)進んで」の意味がある。
＋プラス My watch is five minutes slow. 「私の腕時計は5分遅れている」のように、「(時計が)遅れて」には slow を用いることもここで押さえておこう。

No. 1415 Sending flowers to the funeral parlor would be the ( ) thing to do. ① accurate ② correct ③ exact ④ precise 〈慶應義塾大〉
1415 the correct thing (to do) 「…(するのに)適切なこと」[発展]
▶correct には「適切な/正しい」の意味がある。the correct thing は慣用的な表現。the correct thing to do 「…するのに適切なこと」や the correct thing 「適切なことをする」で押さえておこう。
▶① accurate 「正確な/精密な」、③ exact 「正確な/きっかりの」、④ precise 「正確な/精密な」

No. 1416 Do not rely on the room clock for the ( ) time of day. ① good ② exact ③ most ④ explicit 〈慶應義塾大〉
1416 the exact time (of day) 「正確な時間」[標準]
▶exact には「正確な/きっかりの」の意味がある。the exact time 「正確な時間」、the exact date 「正確な日付」、the exact sum 「正確な額」などで覚えておこう。

No. 1417 "Excuse me, is this seat taken?" "No. It's ( )." ① open ② unseated ③ occupied ④ free 〈愛知学院大〉
1417 This seat is free. 「この席は空いている」[標準]
▶free には「(場所が)空いて/ふさがっていない」の意味がある。
▶① open 「開いて」、② unseated 「ふるい落とされて/議席を奪われて」、③ occupied 「ふさがって」

No. 1418 After he retired, the post remained ( ) for three months. ① absent ② blank ③ free ④ vacant 〈桃山学院大〉
1418 vacant 「(職・地位などが)空位の/欠員になって」[標準]
＋プラス vacant は、本問の用法以外に「(場所が)空いて/使用されてなくて」(=free)の意味も重要。This seat is vacant. (この席は空いています)

No. 1419 "Do you have a single room for tonight?" "Yes, we have one ( )." ① available ② conceivable ③ helpful ④ useful 〈学習院大〉
1419 available 「利用できて/入手できて」[標準]
▶available は「利用できて/入手できて」の意味を表す。本問の available は a single room を指す one を後置修飾している。
▶② conceivable 「考えられる/ありそうな」、③ helpful 「役に立って/有益な」、④ useful 「有益な/有用な」

No. 1420 The firefighter barely escaped death at the fire. = The firefighter had a ( ) escape from death at the fire. ① narrow ② quick ③ short ④ clean 〈関西学院大〉
1420 have a narrow escape from A 「Aを間一髪でのがれる」[標準]
▶narrow には「狭い」の他にも、通例、限定用法(名詞修飾)で「かろうじての/やっとの」の意味がある。
＋プラス この narrow を用いた表現、a narrow victory 「辛勝」、a narrow defeat 「惜敗」、a narrow majority 「ぎりぎりの過半数」なども覚えておこう。

No. 1421 Something's wrong with the car! We must have a ( ) tire. ① broken ② dead ③ flat ④ weak 〈センター試験〉
1421 a flat tire 「パンクした[空気の抜けた]タイヤ」[標準]
▶flat には「平らな」の他にも「(タイヤなどが)空気の抜けた」の意味がある。

No. 1422 The rent is ( ) tomorrow but I have no money in my bank account. ① coming ② due ③ paying ④ ready 〈学習院大〉
1422 The rent is due tomorrow. 「家賃は明日が支払期日である」[標準]
▶due には「支払期日の/満期の」の意味がある。A is due...の形で「Aは…が支払期日である」の意味を表す。(→1359)

No. 1423 In the city library, I happened to find a book with some pages ( ). Fortunately, they were not the pages I needed to photocopy. ① losing ② lost ③ missed ④ missing 〈神奈川大〉
1423 a book with some pages missing 「何ページかがなくなっている本」[標準]
▶「欠けている/あるべきところにない」の意味では missing を用いる。
▶② lost は不可。lost は「失われた/紛失した」の意味であり、lost memory 「失われた記憶」、a lost key 「紛失した鍵」などとは言うが、some lost pages とは言わない。
＋プラス missing, lost ともに「行方不明の」の意味があることも重要。my missing [lost] dog 「行方不明の私のイヌ」

No. 1424 Roger is a ( ) person; he can easily adapt to new circumstances. ① flexible ② frightening ③ simple ④ stubborn 〈京都外大〉
1424 a flexible person 「順応性のある人」[標準]
▶② frightening 「ぎょっとさせるような」、③ simple 「単純な」、④ stubborn 「頑固な」

No. 1425 Jimmy is ( ), being open and honest in stating what he thinks or wants. ① frank ② modest ③ shy ④ kind 〈京都外大〉
1425 frank 「ざっくばらんな/率直な」[標準]
▶② modest 「控え目な」、③ shy 「内気な」、④ kind 「親切な」

No. 1426 Chris is very friendly and ( ), so she is liked by her classmates. ① outgoing ② moody ③ gloomy ④ jealous 〈学習院大〉
1426 outgoing 「社交的な/外向的な」[標準]
▶② moody 「気分の変わりやすい」、③ gloomy 「陰気な」、④ jealous 「しっと深い」

No. 1427 Sarah is always able to answer the teacher's questions. She is such a ( ) girl. ① dependent ② lazy ③ shy ④ smart 〈センター試験〉
1427 smart 「利口な/頭のよい」[標準]
▶① dependent 「依存して」、② lazy 「怠けて」、③ shy 「内気な」

No. 1428 The maid was so ( ) that we dismissed her. ① cheerful ② lazy ③ diligent ④ earnest 〈京都外大〉
1428 lazy 「怠惰な/怠けて」[標準]
▶① cheerful 「元気のいい」、③ diligent 「勤勉な」、④ earnest 「まじめな」

No. 1429 Don't be so ( ). Try to think more flexibly and take into account other people's opinions. ① obstinate ② shy ③ slow ④ timid 〈京都外大〉
1429 obstinate 「頑固な/強情な」[標準]
▶obstinate は「頑固な/強情な」の意味を表す。stubborn「頑固な」とほぼ同意。
▶② shy 「内気な」、③ slow 「鈍い」、④ timid 「臆病な」
!!注意 take A into account 「Aを考慮に入れる」のAが into account の後に移動した形となっている。(→1022)

No. 1430 Tom is very ( ); he is always well-mannered and is considerate of other people's feelings and needs. ① curious ② idle ③ polite ④ rude 〈京都外大〉
1430 polite 「礼儀正しい」[標準]
▶① curious 「好奇心の強い」、② idle 「怠けて」、④ rude 「無礼な」
＋プラス 本問中の be considerate of A は「Aに理解がある/Aに思いやりがある」の意味。(→p.233[整理74])

No. 1431 次の( )に共通する語を入れなさい。
(a) The shop clerk gave me 200 yen in ( ).
(b) I want to ( ) the day of the meeting.
1431 (a) change は名詞で「つり銭/小銭」の意味(→1386)。change を用いた慣用表現 Keep the change. 「おつりはとっておいてください」は頻出。(→1279)
(b) change は動詞で「…を変更する」の意味。

No. 1432 (a) Oh, the girls look so ( ) in those pink dresses.
(b) I was ( ) tired after walking all day.
1432 (a) pretty は形容詞で「かわいい」の意味。
(b) pretty は副詞で「かなり」の意味。(→694) [標準]

No. 1433 (a) This pen isn't ( ). It belongs to Susan.
(b) A few years ago many people were rescued alive from a ( ) accident in Chile.
(c) The researchers developed a robot with the ability to remove a land ( ).
1433 (a) mine は所有代名詞で「私のもの」の意味。
(b) mine は名詞で「鉱坑、鉱山」の意味。
(c) mine は名詞で「地雷、機雷」の意味(= landmine)。 [標準]

No. 1434 (a) The boss will ( ) you if you don't work harder.
(b) The photo albums were burned in the ( ).
1434 (a) fire は動詞で「…を解雇する」の意味。同意語の dismiss と一緒に覚えておこう。
(b) fire は名詞で「火事」の意味。 [標準]

No. 1435 (a) I haven't read that ( ) by Ms. Rowling yet.
(b) Let's ( ) the plane tickets today.
1435 (a) book は名詞で「本」の意味。
(b) book は動詞で「…を予約する」の意味。reserve と同意。 [標準]

No. 1436 (a) Roger opened a ( ) of tuna.
(b) ( ) you play the violin?
1436 (a) can は名詞で「缶」の意味。
(b) can は助動詞で「…できる」の意味。 [標準]

No. 1437 (a) We visited the ( ) of our grandparents in the cemetery.
(b) She had a ( ) expression on her face.
1437 (a) grave は名詞で「墓」の意味。
(b) grave は形容詞で「(顔つき・態度などが)重々しい/深刻な」の意味。 [発展]

No. 1438 (a) My sister works at a publishing ( ) in New York.
(b) Can you keep my dog ( ) until I get back?
1438 (a) company は名詞で「会社」の意味。
(b) company は名詞で「同伴」の意味。keep A company で「Aと一緒にいる」の意味を表す。 [標準]
No.1439 (a) If you hit the glass with a hammer, it will ( ) easily.
(b) Let's take a ten-minute ( ) before we start working again.
(a) break は動詞で「割れる／こわれる」の意味。
(b) break は名詞で「休憩」の意味。 標準

No.1440 (a) In some countries people do not have the ( ) to vote.
(b) The question was so difficult that only a few students found the ( ) answer.
(a) right は名詞で「権利」の意味。
(b) right は形容詞で「正しい」の意味。 標準

No.1441 (a) The opposition parties took a strong ( ) against raising taxes.
(b) The teacher asked all the students to ( ) up and bow.
(c) There is a big supermarket where the hotel used to ( ).
(d) He couldn't ( ) her rude behavior.
(a) stand は名詞で「立場」の意味。
(b) stand は動詞で、stand up は「起立する」の意味。
(c) stand は動詞で「立っている」の意味。
(d) stand は動詞で「…をがまんする」の意味。この意味では否定文のみで使う。 発展

No.1442 (a) She went to bed at eleven and was ( ) asleep by midnight.
(b) Two of those movies ( ) interesting.
(a) sound は副詞で、asleep を修飾して「ぐっすりと」の意味を表す。標準
sound asleep「熟睡して」はイディオムとして押さえる。 (→ 885)
(b) sound は動詞で、sound+形容詞は「…に聞こえる／…のようである」の意味。

No.1443 (a) You must be ( ) to animals and never hurt them.
(b) I'm sorry, we don't have that ( ) of shampoo in this store.
(a) kind は形容詞で「優しい」の意味。
(b) kind は名詞で「種類」の意味。 標準

No.1444 (a) Please give me a ( ) at my office tomorrow.
(b) Sushi is a food which the Japanese can ( ) their own.
(a) call は名詞で「電話」の意味。give A a call で「Aに電話をする」の意味を表す。give A a ring と同意。 (→ p.256[整理85]) 標準
(b) call は動詞で、call O C は「OをCと言う／呼ぶ」の意味。

No.1445 (a) The problem of crows eating garbage is really getting out of ( ).
(b) I have to ( ) him this document by tomorrow.
(c) Can you give me a ( ) to move this table?
(a) hand は名詞で、get out of hand は「手に負えなくなる」の意味を表す。 (→ 1168) 発展
(b) hand は動詞で「…を手渡す／渡す」の意味。
(c) hand は名詞で「手助け／人手」の意味。この意味では常に単数形で使う。

No.1446 (a) Please take off your coat and make yourself at ( ).
(b) The novel brought ( ) to me the meaning of true friendship.
(a) home は名詞で、at home は「くつろいで」=comfortable の意味。 (→ 1145)。make oneself at home 「くつろぐ」は頻出表現。 (→ 269) 標準
(b) home は副詞で「十分に／痛烈に」の意味。bring home to B A [bring A home to B] で「AのことをBにしみじみわからせる」の意味。 (→ 1059)

No.1447 (a) This computer uses a good ( ) of electricity.
(b) The government must ( ) with the problem of traffic jams.
(a) deal は名詞で「量」の意味。a good [great] deal of A (不可算名詞) で「たくさんのA／多量のA」の意味を表す。 (→ 649) 標準
(b) deal は動詞で、deal with A は「Aを扱う／Aに対処する」の意味。 (→ 825)

No.1448 (a) Beethoven has a special ( ) in music history.
(b) Be careful when you ( ) the CD on the tray.
(c) This is a good ( ) to buy used clothes.
(a) place は名詞で「(社会的な)地位、身分」の意味。
(b) place は動詞で「…を(ある位置に)置く」の意味。
(c) place は名詞で「場所」の意味。 標準

No.1449 (a) He told me the ( ) to the bank.
(b) A crying baby will always get his or her ( ).
(c) This is the American ( ) of living.
(a) way は名詞で「道順」の意味。
(b) way は名詞で「やり方」の意味。get [have] one’s (own) way は「自分の思いどおりにする」というイディオム。 (→ 1045) 標準
(c) way は名詞で、「やり方」から派生した「様式／風習」の意味。

No.1450 (a) The beach was ( ) enough to play soccer on.
(b) Unfortunately, my bicycle has a ( ) tire.
(c) Liz lives in a small ( ) in London.
(a) flat は形容詞で「平らな」の意味。
(b) flat は形容詞で「(タイヤなどが)空気の抜けた」の意味。a flat tire「パンクしたタイヤ」で押さえておく。 (→ 1421) 発展
(c) flat はイギリス用法の名詞で「アパート」の意味。

No.1451 (a) It seems to be my ( ) in life.
(b) There is a parking ( ) behind the store.
(c) This math problem is a ( ) easier than that one.
(a) lot は名詞で「運命」の意味。
(b) lot は名詞で「(土地の)一区画」の意味。a parking lot で「駐車場」の意味を表す。 発展
(c) a lot は比較級の強調表現で「はるかに…」の意味を表す。 (→ p.77[整理20])

No.1452 (a) She ( ) become president of the company next year.
(b) My grandfather wrote his ( ) before he died.
(c) She seemed to have lost her ( ) to live.
(a) will は未来を表す助動詞で「…だろう」の意味。
(b) will は名詞で「遺言(書)」の意味。 標準
(c) will は名詞で「意欲／意志」の意味。

No.1453 (a) You can drink the water from the ( ).
(b) She is in the hospital, but I’m sure she’ll get ( ) soon.
(c) Masako speaks French ( ).
(a) well は名詞で「井戸」の意味。
(b) well は形容詞で「健康で」の意味。get well で「元気になる」の意味を表す。 標準
(c) well は副詞で「上手に」の意味。

No.1454 (a) Do you have anything in ( )?
(b) You must be out of your ( )!
(c) Would you ( ) closing the door, please?
(a) mind は名詞で「考え」の意味。have A in mind で「Aを計画中 [考慮中] である」の意味を表す。Do you have anything in mind? 「(買い物などで)何かお考えのものはありますか」は頻出表現。 (→ 1278) 標準
(b) mind は名詞で「理性／正気」の意味。out of one's mind で「正気を失って」の意味を表す。
(c) mind は動詞で「…を嫌がる」の意味。Would you mind doing...? 「…していただけませんか」は重要表現。 (→ 515)

No.1455 (a) That will ( ) more harm than good.
(b) Any ballpoint pen will ( ).
(c) She had nothing to ( ) with the crime.
(a) do は他動詞。do harm で「害になる」、do good で「ためになる」の意味(→ 573, 574)。本問の do more harm than good 「ためになるよりも害になる」も頻出表現。 標準
(b) do は自動詞で「間に合う／十分である」の意味。 (→ 584)
(c) have nothing to do with A 「Aと何の関係もない」は慣用表現として押さえる。 (→ 264)

No.1456 (a) Can you ( ) out the problem to me?
(b) There is no ( ) in crying about it.
(c) Try to understand his ( ) of view.
(a) point は動詞で、point out A は「Aを指摘する」の意味。 標準
(b) point は名詞で「目的／意味」の意味。There is no point (in) doing ... 「…してもむだである」は頻出表現。 (→ 140)
(c) point は名詞で「要点」の意味。A's point of view 「Aの観点」は重要表現。

No.1457 (a) We hope the discovery will serve a useful ( ).
(b) My office is at the ( ) of the hall.
(c) The book has been a best seller for years on ( ).
(d) If you don’t eat healthier food, you will ( ) up sick.
(a) end は名詞で「目的」の意味。同義語の purpose, aim, object と一緒に覚えておこう。 発展
(b) end は名詞で「端／突き当たり」の意味。
(c) on end 「続けて」=continuously はイディオムとして押さえる。 (→ 1146)
(d) end は動詞で、end up + C [形容詞・名詞] は「最後には…になる」の意味を表す。end up (by) doing 「…することで終わる」も一緒に覚えておこう。

No.1458 (a) He gave his personal opinion at the meeting from a ( ) point of view.
(b) They played a ( ) role in the success of the project.
(c) The doctor looks serious today because one of her patients is in ( ) condition.
(a) critical は形容詞で「批判的な」の意味。
(b) critical は形容詞で「重要な」の意味。
(c) critical は形容詞で「危機的な」の意味。 標準

No.1459 (a) The curtain had an ( ) pattern of flowers.
(b) He would not ( ) on the reason for his absence.
(a) elaborate は形容詞で「手の込んだ／複雑な」の意味。
(b) elaborate は動詞で「詳しく述べる」の意味。 標準

No.1460 (a) Can you clear the ( )?
(b) The figures of births in this city last year are shown in the ( ) above.
(a) table は名詞で「テーブル」の意味。
(b) table は名詞で「表」の意味。「下の表に」は in the table below と言う。 標準

No.1461 (a) Global warming is a very important ( ) for the world.
(b) I read an interesting article about nuclear power in the latest ( ) of the magazine.
(c) The company is going to ( ) a press release announcing a new product tomorrow.
(a) issue は名詞で「問題点」の意味。
(b) issue は名詞で「(雑誌などの)号」の意味。
(c) issue は動詞で「…を発行する／発表する」の意味。 標準

No.1462 (a) A service charge is included in the ( ).
(b) Can you change a 10 dollar ( ) into singles?
(c) A new tax ( ) was passed by Congress yesterday.
(a) bill は名詞で「請求書／勘定書」の意味。
(b) bill は名詞で「紙幣」の意味。
(c) bill は名詞で「法案」の意味。 標準

No.1463 (a) It would be better for us to accept his offer in this ( ).
(b) The police are investigating the ( ) as a murder.
(a) case は名詞で「状況／場合」の意味。
(b) case は名詞で「事件」の意味。 標準

No.1464 (a) There is ( ) evidence for his guilt.
(b) We enjoyed good food at a ( ) price at the Italian restaurant.
(a) reasonable は形容詞で「妥当な／合理的な」の意味。
(b) reasonable は形容詞で「手ごろな」の意味。 標準

No.1465 (a) I ( ) I should arrive there by 2:30.
(b) Please look at ( ) 3 which shows yearly imports of corn.
(c) The unemployment ( ) is the lowest in ten years.
(a) figure は動詞で「…と考える／判断する」の意味。
(b) figure は名詞で「図／図表」の意味。
(c) figure は名詞で「数値」の意味。 標準

No.1466 (a) I paid a 100-dollar ( ) for speeding.
(b) We can see a ( ) view from this hotel.
(a) fine は名詞で「罰金」の意味。
(b) fine は形容詞で「立派な／すばらしい」の意味。 標準

No.1467 (a) I have to ( ) my house at 6:00 a.m. for Osaka.
(b) In Japan, employees usually have sixteen weeks of maternity ( ).
(a) leave は動詞で「…を出発する」の意味。
(b) leave は名詞で「休暇／休暇期間」の意味。 標準

No.1468 (a) She is notorious for being ( ) to everyone.
(b) What does “omotenashi” ( ) in English?
(a) mean は形容詞で「意地の悪い／卑劣な」の意味。
(b) mean は動詞で「…を意味する」の意味。 標準

No.1469 (a) The theater is only one ( ) from the station on foot.
(b) The print is so ( ) that it is difficult to read.
(a) minute は名詞で「分」の意味。
(b) minute は形容詞で「微小な」の意味。発音に注意。 標準

No.1470 (a) Names in the data base are in alphabetical ( ).
(b) What did the president ( ) him to do?
(a) order は名詞で「順序／順番」の意味。
(b) order は動詞で「…を命じる」の意味。 標準

No.1471 (a) In the United Kingdom, people always ( ) “realize” with an “s.”
(b) After a short ( ) of fine weather we had a heavy snow.
(c) The professor always insists on the need for inflation to stimulate economy as if it were a magic ( ).
(a) spell は動詞で「(単語)をつづる」の意味。
(b) spell は名詞で「期間」の意味。
(c) spell は名詞で「呪文」の意味。 標準

No.1472 (a) First, can you ( ) your full name and phone number?
(b) Those who live here can enter the ( ) university with a small tuition fee.
(c) The company has been in a bad ( ) for a couple of years because of the recession.
(a) state は動詞で「…を述べる」の意味。
(b) state は名詞で「州」の意味。
(c) state は名詞で「状態」の意味。 標準

No.1473 (a) The TV drama was based on a true ( ) from World War II.
(b) Her apartment is on the ninth ( ).
(a) story は名詞で「物語」の意味。
(b) story は名詞で「階」の意味。 標準

No.1474 (a) If I could find her ( ), I would send her an invitation to the party.
(b) The professor gave an ( ) at the ceremony.
(c) We need to ( ) the problem of climate change now.
(a) address は名詞で「住所」の意味。
(b) address は名詞で「演説」の意味。
(c) address は動詞で「…に取り組む」の意味。 標準
